			  participant_lists.participant_id,

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1
		---------

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 98
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1

			SELECT 
			  participant_lists.participant_id,
			  participant_lists.id,
			  participant_lists.participant_reply_id
			FROM
			  participant_lists
			  
			WHERE
			  participant_lists.session_id = 103
			  AND participant_lists.participant_reply_id=1
